          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="The 100 Dumbest Things Ever Said in Sports" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/608/hi-res-5252410_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Rick Osentoski-USA TODAY Sports
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_info team-color-border cf">
           <div class="total-reads article-stats">
            <div class="team-color-text article-stats_count">
             245.7K
            </div>
            <div class="article-stats_label">
             Reads
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="article_comments js-open-comments article-stats ">
            <div class="comments-count team-color-text article-stats_count">
             73
            </div>
            <div class="comments-label article-stats_label">
             Comments
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Your jaw flops. Your eyes widen. Your hand slaps reflexively onto your forehead.
           </p>
           <p>
            You just heard someone say something very,
            <em>
             very
            </em>
            dumb.
           </p>
           <p>
            But hey, a little slip of the tongue happens to the best of us. And unlike people in the micd up world of sports, we can at least log onto the Internet without seeing our gaffes thrown on a hulking 100-slide feast of face-palm moments.
           </p>
           <p>
            Sports figures, however, have every misguided word they've ever said recorded, carbon copied and seared into the web for all to see.
           </p>
           <p>
            And in keeping with that time-honored tradition, the following is a countdown of the 100 dumbestand funniest, in some casesthings ever uttered in the world of sports.They're everything from innocent slip-ups to intensely misguided musings on paleontology.
           </p>
           <p>
            And trust methey don't all deserve the benefit of the doubt.
           </p>
          </div>

           Begin Slideshow

           </span>
          </a>
         </section>

Dizzy Dean Thought It Was Pretty Close" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/620/DizzyDean_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            </h2>

Dick Vitale Says a Dick Vitale Thing" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/649/hi-res-150881953_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            </h2>
           </div>

            <img alt="92. Steve Largent Will Sincerely Miss Ringo" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/636/hi-res-328701_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1126889/index.htm">

            </a>

           </div>

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            That picture was taken
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/2004/magazine/09/21/si50_tsi0927/">
             out of context
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            -- New York Mets pitcher Jeff Innis on a photo of him that he believed made him look goofy.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             78. Mario BalotelliThe Artless Dodger
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="78. Mario BalotelliThe Artless Dodger" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/703/hi-res-161683730_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">

           </p>

Alex Rodriguez Feels Dominican" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/628/hi-res-154351518_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             70. RMFRandy Moss Financial (LLC)
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="70. RMFRandy Moss Financial (LLC)" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/656/hi-res-160430443_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Scott Halleran/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            When youre rich you dont write checks...
            <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=07G23zMGa4g">
             straight cash
            </a>
            , homey.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Randy Moss when asked how hell pay an NFL fine for unsportsmanlike celebration.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             69. Jerome James Is Selflessly Selfish
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="69. Jerome James Is Selflessly Selfish" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/645/hi-res-52969410_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Otto Greule Jr/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Former Seattle SuperSonics center Jerome James explained his personal views on coach Nate McMillan calling him selfish with this
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1028040/index.htm">
             little ditty
            </a>
            :
           </p>
           <p>
            I dont have the first clue who he is talking about, because all I worry about is Jerome.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             68. Jerry Coleman and the Tale of Two Ex-Teammates
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:541px">
            <img alt="68. Jerry Coleman and the Tale of Two Ex-Teammates" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/622/JerryColeman2_crop_north.jpg?w=541&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="541"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="541">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="541">
             <span itemprop="caption">
              Image via chronicle.augusta.com
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Gaylord Perry and
            <span style="line-height: 1;">
             Willie M
            </span>
            <span style="line-height: 1;">
             cCovey should know each other like a book. Theyve been
             <a href="http://www.baseball-almanac.com/quotes/quocole.shtml">
              ex-teammates
             </a>
             for years now.
            </span>
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Jerry Coleman, San Diego Padres broadcaster
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             67. Bill CowherOrchestral Savant
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="67. Bill CowherOrchestral Savant" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/655/hi-res-72648082_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

           </p>

            on the gridiron.

             66. Lou Holtz Brings the Wood
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">

Lou Holtz Brings the Wood" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/691/hi-res-6921076_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             65. Soccer Manager Botches the Numbers
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:280px">
            <img alt="65. Soccer Manager Botches the Numbers" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/671/RuudGullit_crop_north.jpg?w=280&amp;h=390&amp;q=75" height="390" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="280"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="280">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="280">
             <span itemprop="caption">
              Image via girlslovesoccertoo.wordpress.com
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            We must have had
            <a href="http://www.topdrawersoccer.com/the91stminute/tag/ruud-gullit/">
             99 percent
            </a>
            of the match. It was the other three percent that cost us.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Dutch soccer manager Ruud Gullit
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             64. Shaq Strikes Back
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="64. Shaq Strikes Back" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/699/hi-res-108801897_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">

            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1107553/index.htm">
             idiot
            </a>

            <em>

             63. Terrell Owens Teammate Issues
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="63. Terrell Owens Teammate Issues" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/670/hi-res-6048420_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">

             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Dont say I dont get along with my teammates. I just dont get along with some of the guys on my team.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former NFL wide receiver Terrell Owens
           </p>
          </div>

            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>

Don Kings Interesting Sense of Time" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/680/hi-res-5769034_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             61. Rocky BridgesNot a Slow Eater
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:183px">
            <img alt="61. Rocky BridgesNot a Slow Eater" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/634/RockyBridges_crop_north.jpg?w=183&amp;h=275&amp;q=75" height="275" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="183"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="183">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="183">
             <span itemprop="caption">
              Image via ootpdevelopments.com
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Former San Francisco Giants coach Rocky Bridges was asked why he refused to eat snails, to which he
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1119918/index.htm">
             responded
            </a>
            :
           </p>
           <p>
            I prefer fast food.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             60. Lawrence Taylor Is More of a Poet
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="60. Lawrence Taylor Is More of a Poet" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/637/hi-res-120974668_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Tom Berg/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Its going to be about me.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former NFL great Lawrence Taylor
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1126889/index.htm">
             describing the autobiography
            </a>
            he planned to write.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             51. Joe Theismanns Thoughts on Geniuses
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="51. Joe Theismanns Thoughts on Geniuses" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/641/hi-res-160514961_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Stephen Lovekin/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The word
            <em>
             genius
            </em>
            isnt applicable in football. A genius is a guy like
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1003458/3/index.htm">
             Norman Einstein
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former Washington Redskins quarterback Joe Theisman
           </p>
           <p>
            <em>
             Note:After making this genius quote, Theismann later claimed he was referring to a buddy from high school. You know, that Norman guy we all know about.
            </em>
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             50. Yogi Berra Breaks Down the Game of Baseball
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="50. Yogi Berra Breaks Down the Game of Baseball" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/619/hi-res-94459945_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Jim McIsaac/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Ninety percent of this game is
            <a href="http://www.baseball-almanac.com/quotes/quoberra.shtml">
             half mental
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Yankess legend Yogi Berra
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

Lou WhitakerNo More Taxi Cabs for Your Boy" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/675/hi-res-72527811_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             41. Kellen WinslowNot a Soldier
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="41. Kellen WinslowNot a Soldier" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/660/hi-res-2733016_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">

             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Its war. Theyre out there to kill you, so Im out there to kill them. We dont care about nobody but this U...
            <a href="http://sports.espn.go.com/ncf/news/story?id=1657901">
             Im a soldier
            </a>
            !
           </p>
           <p>
            -- University of Miami tight end Kellen Winslow after a loss to Tennessee in 2003
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             39. Tim McCarver Sets All of Humanity Back Years
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="39. Tim McCarver Sets All of Humanity Back Years" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/666/hi-res-150181312_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Sportscaster Tim McCarver on
            <a href="http://hardballtalk.nbcsports.com/2012/04/30/quote-of-the-weekend-tim-mccarver-explains-increased-home-run-rates/">
             increased home run rates
            </a>
            in the MLB:
           </p>
           <p>
            It has not been proven, but I think it will be proven that the air is thinner now, there have been climactic changes over the last 50 years in the world, and I think thats one of the reasons balls are carrying much better now than I remember.
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             30. Stevie Johnson Tweets God
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="30. Stevie Johnson Tweets God" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/690/hi-res-6670898_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Mark J. Rebilas-USA TODAY Sports
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            "I PRAISE YOU 24/7!!!!!! AND THIS HOW YOU DO ME!!!!! YOU EXPECT ME TO LEARN FROM THIS??? HOW???!!! ILL NEVER FORGET THIS!! EVER!!! THX THO..."
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Buffalo Bills wide receiver Stevie Johnson
            <a href="http://www.nydailynews.com/sports/football/steve-johnson-buffalo-bills-wideout-blames-god-twitter-dropping-game-winning-pass-article-1.456341">
             tweeted
            </a>
            this message, presumably to the creator of the universe, after dropping a game-winning catch in 2010.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="29. Terry Bradshaw Makes a Valid Point" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/674/hi-res-85935186_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Joe Murphy/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I may
            <a href="http://voices.yahoo.com/the-dumbest-things-ever-said-sports-8712665.html?cat=14">
             be dumb
            </a>
            , but Im not stupid.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former NFL great and current NFL analyst Terry Bradshaw.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             28. What a Real Man Looks Like
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">

What a Real Man Looks Like" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/623/hi-res-6191930_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             27. Rickey HendersonOne-Percenter
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="27. Rickey HendersonOne-Percenter" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/687/hi-res-1350021_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

             claim
            </a>
            that 50 percent of major league baseball players use steroids:

            Well, Im not one of them. So thats 49 percent right there."
           </p>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             24. Mike Greenwell and the Family Trucks
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="24. Mike Greenwell and the Family Trucks" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/676/hi-res-1405665_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Stephen Dunn/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Im a four-wheel-drive pickup type of guy, and
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1007828/index.htm">
             so is my wife
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former Red Sox outfielder Mike Greenwell
           </p>
           <p>
            What he probably meant: Im man enough to admit my wife likes mudding trucks and that I dont always get to be the big spoon.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             23. Tim McCarverClearly on Autopilot
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="23. Tim McCarverClearly on Autopilot" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/677/hi-res-150181311_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Hunter Martin/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
             <span itemprop="caption">
              Tim McCarver (pictured middle-left)
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            When San Francisco Giants fans began
            <a href="http://www.usatoday.com/story/gameon/2012/10/24/tim-mccarver-recalls-giants-great-barry-manilow/1656041/">
             chanting
            </a>
            Barry! Barry! Barry! for Giants pitcher Barry Zito in Game 1 of the 2012 World series, broadcaster Joe Buck set up fellow sportscaster Tim McCarver for an easy home run:
           </p>
           <p>
            They used to say [Barry] for somebody else around here, said Buck.
           </p>
           <p>
            When Barry Manilow was playing in a concert, replied McCarver.
           </p>
           <p>
            Or Barry Bonds, said Buck, incredulous.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

             22. Dan Osinski Cant Eat All That Pizza
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:183px">
            <img alt="22. Dan Osinski Cant Eat All That Pizza" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/647/DanOsinski_crop_north.jpg?w=183&amp;h=275&amp;q=75" height="275" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="183"/>

            </a>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             20. George Rogers Isnt in a Rush
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:199px">
            <img alt="20. George Rogers Isnt in a Rush" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/681/GeorgeRogers_crop_north.jpg?w=199&amp;h=253&amp;q=75" height="253" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="199"/>

            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1121110/index.htm">

            </a>
            whichever comes first.

           <p>

            </h2>

          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:313px">
            <img alt="19. Bobby Robsons Miscalculated Miscalculation" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/700/BobbyRobson_crop_north.jpg?w=313&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="313"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="313">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="313">
             <span itemprop="caption">
              Image via dailymail.co.uk
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            We didnt
            <a href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/funny_old_game/8186022.stm">
             underestimate
            </a>
            them. They were a lot better than we thought.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former English football manager Bobby Robson, on narrowly surviving a game against Cameroon in the 1990 World Cup.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             15. Jared Allen Catches Case of the Schisms
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="15. Jared Allen Catches Case of the Schisms" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/692/hi-res-6748088_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

           </p>

            <a href="http://www.sbnation.com/2009/8/28/1644523/vikings-dont-know-the-meaning-of">

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             11. Bobby Hurley Should Stick to Basketball
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="11. Bobby Hurley Should Stick to Basketball " data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/643/hi-res-1396741_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Otto Greule Jr/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Brother Ray Page, a teacher at St. Anthony High School in Jersey City, N.J., claims he once
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1006145/index.htm">
             had to explain
            </a>
            a geographical conundrum to his student, Bobby Hurley, who would go on to play for the Sacramento Kings:
           </p>
           <p>
            [Bobby Hurley] once asked me if Beirut was named after that famous baseball player who hit home runs.
           </p>
          </div>

           </p>

            <a href="http://themoderatevoice.com/177569/dennis-rodman-dismisses-north-korea-prison-camps-by-saying-we-do-the-same-things-in-the-u-s/">

           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            My sisters expecting
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/vault/article/magazine/MAG1125156/index.htm">
             a baby
            </a>
            , and I dont know if Im going to be an aunt or an uncle.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- NC State basketball player Chuck Nevitt explaining to his coach why he appeared nervous during practice.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             8. Rashard Mendenhall Likens NFL to Slavery
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="8. Rashard Mendenhall Likens NFL to Slavery" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/695/hi-res-6648416_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Charles LeClaire-USA TODAY Sports
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Anyone with knowledge of the slave trade and the NFL could say that these two parallel each other.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Pittsburgh Steelers running back Rashard Mendenhall
            <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/2011/03/17/rashard-mendenhall-adrian-peterson_n_837180.html">
             tweeted
            </a>
            this nugget of historical wisdom in 2011.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            </h2>
           </div>

            </h2>
           </div>

Bill Cowher Doesn't Want to Skin the Rules" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/654/hi-res-72841155_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             4. Jose Canseco Explains Gravity, Dinosaurs
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="4. Jose Canseco Explains Gravity, Dinosaurs" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/629/hi-res-80556857_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Michael Buckner/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            Never one to hold back on the crazy, Jose Canseco unleashed these
            <a href="http://www.pcmag.com/article2/0,2817,2415604,00.asp">
             dinosaur/physics related tweets
            </a>
            on his followers earlier this month:
           </p>
           <p>
            Ancient gravity was much weaker..."
           </p>
           <p>
            Gravity had to be weaker to make dinosaurs nimble.
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>
         <section class="article_page article_page--secondary js-article-page-99 cf display-none " data-page="99">
          <header class="article_page-header">
           <div class="article_nav-bar br-texture--sudo br-texture--sudo-fade-to-white">
            <div class="paginators paginators--top">

             </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             3. Carl Everett Proves Creationism
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="3. Carl Everett Proves Creationism" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/689/hi-res-57050102_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Stephen Dunn/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The Bible never says anything about dinosaurs.
            <a href="http://sportsillustrated.cnn.com/features/cover/news/2000/07/19/everett_flashback/">
             You can't say
            </a>
            there were dinosaurs when you never saw them. Someone actually saw Adam and Eve. No one ever saw a Tyrannosaurus Rex."
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former MLB outfielder Carl Everett
           </p>
          </div>
         </section>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             2. Mike Cameron, Amateur Astrologist
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="2. Mike Cameron, Amateur Astrologist" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/626/hi-res-110106326_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">

             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            The sun has been there for
            <a href="http://sports.espn.go.com/espn/page2/story?page=simmons/quotes/archive&amp;num=0">
             500, 600 years
            </a>
            .
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Former MLB outfielder Mike Cameron
           </p>
          </div>

            <h2 class="article_page-title" itemprop="alternativeHeadline">
             1. ShaqParthenon VIP
            </h2>
           </div>
          </header>
          <div class="article_image" itemprop="associatedMedia">
           <div class="article_image--main " itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject" style="max-width:630px">
            <img alt="1. ShaqParthenon VIP" data-defer-src="http://img.bleacherreport.net/img/slides/photos/003/019/684/hi-res-162300873_crop_north.jpg?w=630&amp;h=420&amp;q=75" height="420" itemprop="contentURL" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVQIHWNgYAAAAAMAAU9ICq8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" width="630"/>
            <div class="caption-overlay border-box" max-width="630">
            </div>
            <div class="article_image-accreditation" max-width="630">
             <span>
              Harry How/Getty Images
             </span>
             <br/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="article_body cf" itemprop="articleBody">
           <p>
            I cant really remember the names of the clubs that we went to.
           </p>
           <p>
            -- Shaquille ONeals
            <a href="http://sports.espn.go.com/espn/page2/story?page=neumann/110603_shaquille_oneal_retiring&amp;sportCat=nba">
             response
            </a>
            to whether or not he had stopped at the Parthenon while in Greece.
           </p>
